target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-scope="menu" data-part="item" id="_R_2danpfn5tlb_/Open in Claude" role="menuitem" data-ownedby="menu:_R_2danpfn5tlb_:content" data-value="Open in Claude" class="menu__item menu__item--size_sm"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_2 flex-d_row w_full"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" 2.2914 5.9456Z"></path></svg><span>Open in Claude</span></div></a></div></div></div></div><p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">A tree collection is designed to manage hierarchical data structures like file systems, navigation menus, or
organization charts. It provides powerful methods for traversing, manipulating, and querying tree structures.</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">import</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> { createTreeCollection } </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">from</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> &#x27;@ark-ui/react/collection&#x27;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> treeData</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  value: </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;root&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  label: </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;Root&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  children: [</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">      value: </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;folder1&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">      label: </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;Folder 1&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">      children: [</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">        { value: </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;file1&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, label: </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;File 1.txt&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">        { value: </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;file2&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, label: </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;File 2.txt&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">      ],</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">      value: </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;folder2&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">      label: </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;Folder 2&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">      children: [</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">        {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">          value: </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;subfolder1&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">          label: </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;Subfolder 1&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">          children: [{ value: </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;file3&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, label: </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;File 3.txt&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> }],</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">        },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">      ],</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  ],</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> tree</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF"> createTreeCollection</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">({ rootNode: treeData })</span></span></code></pre>
<h3 id="navigation-methods" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#navigation-methods"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Navigation Methods</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">The tree collection provides various methods to navigate through the hierarchical structure.</p>
<h4 id="getting-first-and-last-nodes" class="mt_1.5em mb_0.5em lh_1.5 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#getting-first-and-last-nodes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Getting First and Last Nodes</h4>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> firstNode</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> tree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">getFirstNode</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">()</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">console.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">log</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(firstNode?.value) </span><span style="color:#8B949E">// &quot;folder1&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> lastNode</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> tree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">getLastNode</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">()</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">console.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">log</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(lastNode?.value) </span><span style="color:#8B949E">// &quot;folder2&quot;</span></span></code></pre>
<h4 id="sequential-navigation" class="mt_1.5em mb_0.5em lh_1.5 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#sequential-navigation"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Sequential Navigation</h4>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Navigate to the next or previous node in the tree traversal order:</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> nextNode</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> tree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">getNextNode</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;file1&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">console.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">log</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(nextNode?.value) </span><span style="color:#8B949E">// &quot;file2&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> previousNode</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> tree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">getPreviousNode</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;file2&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">console.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">log</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(previousNode?.value) </span><span style="color:#8B949E">// &quot;file1&quot;</span></span></code></pre>
<h3 id="hierarchical-relationships" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#hierarchical-relationships"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Hierarchical Relationships</h3>
<h4 id="parent-and-children" class="mt_1.5em mb_0.5em lh_1.5 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#parent-and-children"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Parent and Children</h4>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Get parent and descendant nodes:</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E">// Get parent node</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> parentNode</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> tree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">getParentNode</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;file1&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">console.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">log</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(parentNode?.value) </span><span style="color:#8B949E">// &quot;folder1&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E">// Get all ancestor nodes</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> ancestors</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> tree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">getParentNodes</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;file3&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">console.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">log</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(ancestors.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">map</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">((</span><span style="color:#FFA657">n</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">) </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=&gt;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> n.value)) </span><span style="color:#8B949E">// [&quot;folder2&quot;, &quot;subfolder1&quot;]</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E">// Get all descendant nodes</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> descendants</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> tree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">getDescendantNodes</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;folder1&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">console.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">log</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(descendants.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">map</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">((</span><span style="color:#FFA657">n</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">) </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=&gt;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> n.value)) </span><span style="color:#8B949E">// [&quot;file1&quot;, &quot;file2&quot;]</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E">// Get descendant values only</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> descendantValues</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> tree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">getDescendantValues</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;folder2&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">console.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">log</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(descendantValues) </span><span style="color:#8B949E">// [&quot;subfolder1&quot;, &quot;file3&quot;]</span></span></code></pre>
<h4 id="sibling-navigation" class="mt_1.5em mb_0.5em lh_1.5 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#sibling-navigation"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Sibling Navigation</h4>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Navigate between sibling nodes:</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E">// Assuming we have the index path of &quot;file1&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> indexPath</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> tree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">getIndexPath</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;file1&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">) </span><span style="color:#8B949E">// [0, 0]</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> nextSibling</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> tree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">getNextSibling</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(indexPath)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">console.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">log</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(nextSibling?.value) </span><span style="color:#8B949E">// &quot;file2&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> previousSibling</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> tree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">getPreviousSibling</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(indexPath)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">console.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">log</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(previousSibling) </span><span style="color:#8B949E">// undefined (no previous sibling)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E">// Get all siblings</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> siblings</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> tree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">getSiblingNodes</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(indexPath)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">console.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">log</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(siblings.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">map</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">((</span><span style="color:#FFA657">n</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">) </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=&gt;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> n.value)) </span><span style="color:#8B949E">// [&quot;file1&quot;, &quot;file2&quot;]</span></span></code></pre>
<h3 id="index-path-operations" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#index-path-operations"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Index Path Operations</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Work with index paths to identify node positions:</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E">// Get index path for a value</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> indexPath</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> tree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">getIndexPath</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;file3&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">console.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">log</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(indexPath) </span><span style="color:#8B949E">// [1, 0, 0]</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E">// Get value from index path</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> value</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> tree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">getValue</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">([</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">1</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">0</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">0</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">])</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">console.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">log</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(value) </span><span style="color:#8B949E">// &quot;file3&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E">// Get full value path (all ancestors + node)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> valuePath</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> tree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">getValuePath</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">([</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">1</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">0</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">0</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">])</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">console.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">log</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(valuePath) </span><span style="color:#8B949E">// [&quot;folder2&quot;, &quot;subfolder1&quot;, &quot;file3&quot;]</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E">// Get node at specific index path</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> node</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> tree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">at</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">([</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">1</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">0</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">])</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">console.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">log</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(node?.value) </span><span style="color:#8B949E">// &quot;subfolder1&quot;</span></span></code></pre>
<h3 id="tree-queries" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#tree-queries"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Tree Queries</h3>
<h4 id="branch-and-leaf-detection" class="mt_1.5em mb_0.5em lh_1.5 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#branch-and-leaf-detection"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Branch and Leaf Detection</h4>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E">// Check if a node is a branch (has children)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> folder1Node</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> tree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">findNode</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;folder1&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> isBranch</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> tree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">isBranchNode</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(folder1Node</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">!</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">console.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">log</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(isBranch) </span><span style="color:#8B949E">// true</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E">// Get all branch values</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> branchValues</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> tree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">getBranchValues</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">()</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">console.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">log</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(branchValues) </span><span style="color:#8B949E">// [&quot;folder1&quot;, &quot;folder2&quot;, &quot;subfolder1&quot;]</span></span></code></pre>
<h4 id="tree-traversal" class="mt_1.5em mb_0.5em lh_1.5 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#tree-traversal"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Tree Traversal</h4>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Visit all nodes with custom logic:</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">tree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">visit</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#D2A8FF">  onEnter</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: (</span><span style="color:#FFA657">node</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, </span><span style="color:#FFA657">indexPath</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">) </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=&gt;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    console.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">log</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">`Visiting: ${</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">node</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">.</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">value</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">} at depth ${</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">indexPath</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">.</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">length</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">}`</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E">    // Skip certain branches</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">    if</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> (node.value </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">===</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> &#x27;folder2&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">      return</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> &#x27;skip&#x27;</span><span style="color:#8B949E"> // Skip this branch and its children</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">})</span></span></code></pre>
<h4 id="filtering" class="mt_1.5em mb_0.5em lh_1.5 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#filtering"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Filtering</h4>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Create a new tree with filtered nodes:</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E">// Keep only nodes that match criteria</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> filteredTree</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> tree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">filter</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">((</span><span style="color:#FFA657">node</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, </span><span style="color:#FFA657">indexPath</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">) </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=&gt;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">  return</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> node.value.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">includes</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;file&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">) </span><span style="color:#8B949E">// Only keep files</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">})</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">console.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">log</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(filteredTree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">getValues</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">()) </span><span style="color:#8B949E">// [&quot;file1&quot;, &quot;file2&quot;, &quot;file3&quot;]</span></span></code></pre>
<h3 id="tree-manipulation" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#tree-manipulation"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Tree Manipulation</h3>
<h4 id="adding-nodes" class="mt_1.5em mb_0.5em lh_1.5 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#adding-nodes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Adding Nodes</h4>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> newFile</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> { value: </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;newfile&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, label: </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;New File.txt&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> }</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E">// Insert after a specific node</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> indexPath</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> tree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">getIndexPath</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;file1&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> updatedTree</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> tree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">insertAfter</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(indexPath</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">!</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, [newFile])</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E">// Insert before a specific node</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> updatedTree2</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> tree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">insertBefore</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(indexPath</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">!</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, [newFile])</span></span></code></pre>
<h4 id="removing-nodes" class="mt_1.5em mb_0.5em lh_1.5 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#removing-nodes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Removing Nodes</h4>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> indexPath</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> tree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">getIndexPath</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;file2&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> updatedTree</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> tree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">remove</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">([indexPath</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">!</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">])</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">console.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">log</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(updatedTree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">getValues</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">()) </span><span style="color:#8B949E">// file2 is removed</span></span></code></pre>
<h4 id="moving-nodes" class="mt_1.5em mb_0.5em lh_1.5 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#moving-nodes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Moving Nodes</h4>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> fromIndexPaths</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> [tree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">getIndexPath</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;file1&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">)</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">!</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> toIndexPath</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> tree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">getIndexPath</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;folder2&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">)</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">!</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> updatedTree</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> tree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">move</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(fromIndexPaths, toIndexPath)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E">// file1 is now moved under folder2</span></span></code></pre>
<h4 id="replacing-nodes" class="mt_1.5em mb_0.5em lh_1.5 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#replacing-nodes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Replacing Nodes</h4>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> indexPath</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> tree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">getIndexPath</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;file1&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">)</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">!</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> newNode</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> { value: </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;replacedfile&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, label: </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;Replaced File.txt&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> }</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> updatedTree</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> tree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">replace</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(indexPath, newNode)</span></span></code></pre>
<h3 id="utility-methods" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#utility-methods"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Utility Methods</h3>
<h4 id="flattening" class="mt_1.5em mb_0.5em lh_1.5 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#flattening"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Flattening</h4>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Convert the tree to a flat structure:</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> flatNodes</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> tree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">flatten</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">()</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">console.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">log</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(flatNodes.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">map</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">((</span><span style="color:#FFA657">n</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">) </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=&gt;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> ({ value: n.value, depth: n._indexPath.</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">length</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> })))</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#8B949E">// [{ value: &quot;folder1&quot;, depth: 1 }, { value: &quot;file1&quot;, depth: 2 }, ...]</span></span></code></pre>
<h4 id="getting-all-values" class="mt_1.5em mb_0.5em lh_1.5 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#getting-all-values"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Getting All Values</h4>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> allValues</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> tree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">getValues</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">()</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">console.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">log</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(allValues) </span><span style="color:#8B949E">// [&quot;folder1&quot;, &quot;file1&quot;, &quot;file2&quot;, &quot;folder2&quot;, &quot;subfolder1&quot;, &quot;file3&quot;]</span></span></code></pre>
<h4 id="depth-calculation" class="mt_1.5em mb_0.5em lh_1.5 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#depth-calculation"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Depth Calculation</h4>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> depth</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> tree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">getDepth</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;file3&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">console.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">log</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(depth) </span><span style="color:#8B949E">// 3 (root -&gt; folder2 -&gt; subfolder1 -&gt; file3)</span></span></code></pre>
<h3 id="working-with-custom-node-types" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#working-with-custom-node-types"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Working with Custom Node Types</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">You can customize how the tree collection interprets your data:</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">interface</span><span style="color:#FFA657"> CustomNode</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FFA657">  id</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">:</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> string</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FFA657">  name</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">:</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> string</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FFA657">  items</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">?:</span><span style="color:#FFA657"> CustomNode</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">[]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FFA657">  isDisabled</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">?:</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> boolean</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> customTree</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF"> createTreeCollection</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;</span><span style="color:#FFA657">CustomNode</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  rootNode: {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    id: </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;root&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    name: </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;Root&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    items: [</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">      { id: </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;1&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, name: </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;Item 1&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, isDisabled: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">false</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">      { id: </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;2&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, name: </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;Item 2&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, isDisabled: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">true</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    ],</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#D2A8FF">  nodeToValue</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: (</span><span style="color:#FFA657">node</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">) </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=&gt;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> node.id,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#D2A8FF">  nodeToString</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: (</span><span style="color:#FFA657">node</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">) </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=&gt;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> node.name,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#D2A8FF">  nodeToChildren</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: (</span><span style="color:#FFA657">node</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">) </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=&gt;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> node.items,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#D2A8FF">  isNodeDisabled</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: (</span><span style="color:#FFA657">node</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">) </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=&gt;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> node.isDisabled </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">??</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> false</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">})</span></span></code></pre>
<h3 id="creating-trees-from-file-paths" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#creating-trees-from-file-paths"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Creating Trees from File Paths</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Create a tree structure from file paths:</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">import</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> { createFileTreeCollection } </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">from</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> &#x27;@ark-ui/react/collection&#x27;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> paths</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> [</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;src/components/Button.tsx&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;src/components/Input.tsx&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;src/utils/helpers.ts&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">, </span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;docs/README.md&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">]</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">const</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> fileTree</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> =</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF"> createFileTreeCollection</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(paths)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">console.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">log</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(fileTree.</span><span style="color:#D2A8FF">getBranchValues</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">()) </span><span style="color:#8B949E">// [&quot;src&quot;, &quot;components&quot;, &quot;utils&quot;, &quot;docs&quot;]</span></span></code></pre>
<blockquote class="mt_1.6em mb_1.6em ps_1em fw_500 font-style_italic bd-s-w_0.25rem bd-c_var(--colors-prose-quote-border)">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Good to know</strong>: Tree collections are immutable - all modification methods return a new tree instance rather than
modifying the original.</p>
</blockquote></article><div class="d_flex flex-d_column-reverse sm:flex-d_row jc_space-between gap_3"><a class="bdr_lg bd-w_1px d_flex w_full sm:w_50% flex-d_column gap_1.5 p_4 trs-dur_normal hover:c_fg.default [\u0026_svg]:w_5 [\u0026_svg]:h_5\"}]\n"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"29:[\"$\",\"$L2d\",null,{}]\n2f:T1ae0,"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"A tree collection is designed to manage hierarchical data structures like file systems, navigation menus, or\norganization charts. It provides powerful methods for traversing, manipulating, and querying tree structures.\n\n```ts\nimport { createTreeCollection } from '@ark-ui/react/collection'\n\nconst treeData = {\n  value: 'root',\n  label: 'Root',\n  children: [\n    {\n      value: 'folder1',\n      label: 'Folder 1',\n      children: [\n        { value: 'file1', label: 'File 1.txt' },\n        { value: 'file2', label: 'File 2.txt' },\n      ],\n    },\n    {\n      value: 'folder2',\n      label: 'Folder 2',\n      children: [\n        {\n          value: 'subfolder1',\n          label: 'Subfolder 1',\n          children: [{ value: 'file3', label: 'File 3.txt' }],\n        },\n      ],\n    },\n  ],\n}\n\nconst tree = createTreeCollection({ rootNode: treeData })\n```\n\n### Navigation Methods\n\nThe tree collection provides various methods to navigate through the hierarchical structure.\n\n#### Getting First and Last Nodes\n\n```ts\nconst firstNode = tree.getFirstNode()\nconsole.log(firstNode?.value) // \"folder1\"\n\nconst lastNode = tree.getLastNode()\nconsole.log(lastNode?.value) // \"folder2\"\n```\n\n#### Sequential Navigation\n\nNavigate to the next or previous node in the tree traversal order:\n\n```ts\nconst nextNode = tree.getNextNode('file1')\nconsole.log(nextNode?.value) // \"file2\"\n\nconst previousNode = tree.getPreviousNode('file2')\nconsole.log(previousNode?.value) // \"file1\"\n```\n\n### Hierarchical Relationships\n\n#### Parent and Children\n\nGet parent and descendant nodes:\n\n```ts\n// Get parent node\nconst parentNode = tree.getParentNode('file1')\nconsole.log(parentNode?.value) // \"folder1\"\n\n// Get all ancestor nodes\nconst ancestors = tree.getParentNodes('file3')\nconsole.log(ancestors.map((n) =\u003e n.value)) // [\"folder2\", \"subfolder1\"]\n\n// Get all descendant nodes\nconst descendants = tree.getDescendantNodes('folder1')\nconsole.log(descendants.map((n) =\u003e n.value)) // [\"file1\", \"file2\"]\n\n// Get descendant values only\nconst descendantValues = tree.getDescendantValues('folder2')\nconsole.log(descendantValues) // [\"subfolder1\", \"file3\"]\n```\n\n#### Sibling Navigation\n\nNavigate between sibling nodes:\n\n```ts\n// Assuming we have the index path of \"file1\"\nconst indexPath = tree.getIndexPath('file1') // [0, 0]\n\nconst nextSibling = tree.getNextSibling(indexPath)\nconsole.log(nextSibling?.value) // \"file2\"\n\nconst previousSibling = tree.getPreviousSibling(indexPath)\nconsole.log(previousSibling) // undefined (no previous sibling)\n\n// Get all siblings\nconst siblings = tree.getSiblingNodes(indexPath)\nconsole.log(siblings.map((n) =\u003e n.value)) // [\"file1\", \"file2\"]\n```\n\n### Index Path Operations\n\nWork with index paths to identify node positions:\n\n```ts\n// Get index path for a value\nconst indexPath = tree.getIndexPath('file3')\nconsole.log(indexPath) // [1, 0, 0]\n\n// Get value from index path\nconst value = tree.getValue([1, 0, 0])\nconsole.log(value) // \"file3\"\n\n// Get full value path (all ancestors + node)\nconst valuePath = tree.getValuePath([1, 0, 0])\nconsole.log(valuePath) // [\"folder2\", \"subfolder1\", \"file3\"]\n\n// Get node at specific index path\nconst node = tree.at([1, 0])\nconsole.log(node?.value) // \"subfolder1\"\n```\n\n### Tree Queries\n\n#### Branch and Leaf Detection\n\n```ts\n// Check if a node is a branch (has children)\nconst folder1Node = tree.findNode('folder1')\nconst isBranch = tree.isBranchNode(folder1Node!)\nconsole.log(isBranch) // true\n\n// Get all branch values\nconst branchValues = tree.getBranchValues()\nconsole.log(branchValues) // [\"folder1\", \"folder2\", \"subfolder1\"]\n```\n\n#### Tree Traversal\n\nVisit all nodes with custom logic:\n\n```ts\ntree.visit({\n  onEnter: (node, indexPath) =\u003e {\n    console.log(`Visiting: ${node.value} at depth ${indexPath.length}`)\n\n    // Skip certain branches\n    if (node.value === 'folder2') {\n      return 'skip' // Skip this branch and its children\n    }\n  },\n})\n```\n\n#### Filtering\n\nCreate a new tree with filtered nodes:\n\n```ts\n// Keep only nodes that match criteria\nconst filteredTree = tree.filter((node, indexPath) =\u003e {\n  return node.value.includes('file') // Only keep files\n})\n\nconsole.log(filteredTree.getValues()) // [\"file1\", \"file2\", \"file3\"]\n```\n\n### Tree Manipulation\n\n#### Adding Nodes\n\n```ts\nconst newFile = { value: 'newfile', label: 'New File.txt' }\n\n// Insert after a specific node\nconst indexPath = tree.getIndexPath('file1')\nconst updatedTree = tree.insertAfter(indexPath!, [newFile])\n\n// Insert before a specific node\nconst updatedTree2 = tree.insertBefore(indexPath!, [newFile])\n```\n\n#### Removing Nodes\n\n```ts\nconst indexPath = tree.getIndexPath('file2')\nconst updatedTree = tree.remove([indexPath!])\n\nconsole.log(updatedTree.getValues()) // file2 is removed\n```\n\n#### Moving Nodes\n\n```ts\nconst fromIndexPaths = [tree.getIndexPath('file1')!]\nconst toIndexPath = tree.getIndexPath('folder2')!\n\nconst updatedTree = tree.move(fromIndexPaths, toIndexPath)\n// file1 is now moved under folder2\n```\n\n#### Replacing Nodes\n\n```ts\nconst indexPath = tree.getIndexPath('file1')!\nconst newNode = { value: 'replacedfile', label: 'Replaced File.txt' }\n\nconst updatedTree = tree.replace(indexPath, newNode)\n```\n\n### Utility Methods\n\n#### Flattening\n\nConvert the tree to a flat structure:\n\n```ts\nconst flatNodes = tree.flatten()\nconsole.log(flatNodes.map((n) =\u003e ({ value: n.value, depth: n._indexPath.length })))\n// [{ value: \"folder1\", depth: 1 }, { value: \"file1\", depth: 2 }, ...]\n```\n\n#### Getting All Values\n\n```ts\nconst allValues = tree.getValues()\nconsole.log(allValues) // [\"folder1\", \"file1\", \"file2\", \"folder2\", \"subfolder1\", \"file3\"]\n```\n\n#### Depth Calculation\n\n```ts\nconst depth = tree.getDepth('file3')\nconsole.log(depth) // 3 (root -\u003e folder2 -\u003e subfolder1 -\u003e file3)\n```\n\n### Working with Custom Node Types\n\nYou can customize how the tree collection interprets your data:\n\n```ts\ninterface CustomNode {\n  id: string\n  name: string\n  items?: CustomNode[]\n  isDisabled?: boolean\n}\n\nconst customTree = createTreeCollection\u003cCustomNode\u003e({\n  rootNode: {\n    id: 'root',\n    name: 'Root',\n    items: [\n      { id: '1', name: 'Item 1', isDisabled: false },\n      { id: '2', name: 'Item 2', isDisabled: true },\n    ],\n  },\n  nodeToValue: (node) =\u003e node.id,\n  nodeToString: (node) =\u003e node.name,\n  nodeToChildren: (node) =\u003e node.items,\n  isNodeDisabled: (node) =\u003e node.isDisabled ?? false,\n})\n```\n\n### Creating Trees from File Paths\n\nCreate a tree structure from file paths:\n\n```ts\nimport { createFileTreeCollection } from '@ark-ui/react/collection'\n\nconst paths = ['src/components/Button.tsx', 'src/components/Input.tsx', 'src/utils/helpers.ts', 'docs/README.md']\n\nconst fileTree = createFileTreeCollection(paths)\nconsole.log(fileTree.getBranchValues()) // [\"src\", \"components\", \"utils\", \"docs\"]\n```\n\n\u003e **Good to know**: Tree collections are immutable - all modification methods return a new tree instance rather than\n\u003e modifying the original."])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"14:[\"$\",\"div\",null,{\"ref\":\"$undefined\",\"className\":\"pos_relative w_100% max-w_8xl mx_auto px_4 md:px_8 d_flex py_12 gap_8
